5/10/22, 09:24 - +91 95600 29475: from enum import auto
def eval_model(x,y):
  res=list()
  

  cv=RepeatedKFold(n_splits=10,n_repeats=10,random_state=442)
  
  for train,test in cv.split(x):
    x_train,x_test=x[train],x[test]
    y_train,y_test=y[train],y[test]
    print(train.shape)
    print(test.shape)
    
    model=get_model(19,1)
    model.fit(x_train,y_train,verbose=0,epochs=100)
    pred= model.predict(x_test)
  
    acc=accuracy_score(y_test,pred)

    print('>%.3f'%acc)
    res.append(acc)
  return res

res=eval_model(x,y)

print('Accuracy: %.3f (%.3f)' % (mean(res), std(res)))

8/4/22, 21:47 - +91 87501 66010: *Certificates are worthless as well as really important !!*

1. If you want to showcase your skills and tell everyone that I know python because I have a certificate, then certificates are important for you.
1.1 If you want to become a python developer and get a job, certificates are worthless.

2. If you want to brag in front of your college mates, certificates might help you a lot.
2.1 If you want to become better at any skill, the same certificate is worthless.

3. If you want to fill up 50% of your resume with certificates in order to showcase you are talented, certificates will help you to fill up space.
3.1 If you want to fill up your resume with your skills, projects will help. you to showcase not certificates.
There are technical positions where certificates plays an important role, you can learn about them. You can learn more about the usage of certificates, when to add or when to remove in a small video.

https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HR3YLE6pDeU
Open directly in youtube app: https://appopener.com/yt/1rnqs8r60

Do share it with your juniors, they need this guidance a lot ‚ù§Ô∏è

There might be a possibility that person 2 has a better resume. But I have seen the best resumes getting rejected in hundreds of applications.

There are multiple reasons for it:
1. The position might be inactive.
2. Hiring was freezer on that position
3. You applied at the wrong time.
4. The opening was too old and never updated by the recruiter
and much more.
